<div id="review_95366653" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/95366653" />
    <a title="Dahlia (yadkny)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2974366-dahlia-yadkny"><img alt="Dahlia (yadkny)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1337992792p2/2974366.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/95366653?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dahlia (yadkny)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dahlia (yadkny)" href="/user/show/2974366-dahlia-yadkny">Dahlia (yadkny)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Vampire Lovers</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer95366653&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer95366653" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5522712297622494057">I absolutely adore Kade! In the other books you don't really get a sense of who or what Kade and Brock are all about since they are new to the Breed Brotherhood. Since the setting of the story takes place mostly in Alaska you really get a sense of who Kade is and where he started without the drama of the other brothers interfering. Alexandra was also a great addition to the growing number of Breedmates already in the compound and I am proud that we will have another strong female. Her airplane f</span>
  <span id="freeText5522712297622494057" style="display:none">I absolutely adore Kade! In the other books you don't really get a sense of who or what Kade and Brock are all about since they are new to the Breed Brotherhood. Since the setting of the story takes place mostly in Alaska you really get a sense of who Kade is and where he started without the drama of the other brothers interfering. Alexandra was also a great addition to the growing number of Breedmates already in the compound and I am proud that we will have another strong female. Her airplane flying skills are definitely going to come in handy when the females go on another recon mission. Wit Alex's flying/gun handling skills and Renata's driving/fighting skills, they will definitely make an unstoppable duo. Although I don't find that her special talent will really be of any contribution to the war against Dragos. Maybe having a living Breedmate lie detector could come in handy at some point, who knows. Now Kade's talent should definitely come in handy and in fact already has. It was also interesting to read more about the family dynamics of someone who belongs to the Breed. With the other warriors you really don't hear anything of the family they may have left behind in a Darkhaven somewhere. In this instance we find that Kade has somewhat of an evil twin. The relationship dynamics between the two main characters kind of goes as expected where Kade feels that he isn't good enough or honorable enough for Alex and is the first to realize between the two that only what they feel for each other should matter. It actually ends up not taking as much convincing as is usual in this series for Kade to realize that she is right and in fact his fighting his attraction for her doesn't matter since he is already blood bonded to her. I am not sure of how I feel or where the author is going to take the story about Alex's friend Jenna now being involved in the drama. That will have to be left for the next story. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5522712297622494057" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bR7HpxIUZW+mreND9PcoqrTr/+e55jTRmIi2CLQYHvbfuLyadPiqJq0Q20pla79DTvcOaJRdnM48GrYRYP3OZQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pSDPB+Cpw9Uybrb94p0o0qa/Ct75zYBGyHtuNiD4T78XhrQ6hkUMnDnTjvRzAb87XKP7UdR2KFls6W4v9B2fLA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer15390981010190475495"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers hav</span>
  <span id="freeText15390981010190475495" style="display:none"><b>LARA ADRIAN</b> is a <i>New York Times</i> and #1 internationally best-selling author with nearly 4 million books in print and digital worldwide and translations licensed to more than 20 countries. Her books have been named among Amazon’s Top Ten Romances of the Year, and have also been nominated by readers multiple times as finalists for the Goodreads Choice Award for Best Romance of the Year. Reviewers have called Lara’s books “addictively readable” (Chicago Tribune), “extraordinary” (Fresh Fiction), “strikingly original” (Booklist), and “one of the best vampire series on the market” (Romantic Times).<br /> <br />Writing as <b>TINA ST. JOHN</b>, her historical romances have won numerous awards including the National Readers Choice; Romantic Times Magazine Reviewer’s Choice; Booksellers Best; and many others. She was twice named a Finalist in Romance Writers of America’s RITA Awards, for Best Historical Romance (White Lion’s Lady) and Best Paranormal Romance (Heart of the Hunter). More recently, the German translation of Heart of the Hunter debuted on Der Spiegel bestseller list.<br /><br />With an ancestry stretching back to the Mayflower and the court of King Henry VIII, the author lives with her husband in New England, where she is working on her next novel. Visit Lara’s website and sign up for new release announcements at <a href="http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews" rel="nofollow noopener">http://bit.ly/LaraAdrianNews</a><br /></span>
